## Automated Deep Investigation Protocol

1. Reproduce the BA result with the command above before editing code.
2. Inspect the primary evidence file/line for each actionable finding.
3. Classify each finding as confirmed bug, false positive, coverage gap, or intentionally deferred.
4. Treat deterministic/high-confidence scanner failures as likely defects; treat action_feedback_static failures as heuristic suspects requiring confirmation.
5. Implement focused bug fixes only for confirmed defects in the selected app ownership surface.
6. If a BA finding is false positive or too vague to fix safely, report the scanner limitation and recommend a BA scanner improvement instead of changing app code.
7. Run the relevant app verification plus the BA reproduce command after changes.

## Requested Work

1. Read this BA evidence packet and the canonical BA report below.
2. Perform an automated deep investigation using the protocol above.
3. Formulate a targeted fix spec for the selected app only.
4. Perform a double heavy-duty review of the fix plan before editing.
5. Apply focused changes in the selected app owned files only.
6. Run verification and report results back through the mailbox.

## Expected Response Contract

- acknowledge the target app and actionable count.
- summarize confirmed bugs versus false positives, coverage gaps, and deferred findings.
- list the exact finding ids handled or intentionally deferred.
- If any actionable finding is not addressed in the current fix pass, list it exactly as: DEFERRED: [finding title] — [reason]. Silence on a finding is not acceptable and will be treated as an oversight, not a decision.
- include a Finding Disposition section that accounts for every finding in the Finding Index.
- list touched files.
- provide verification commands and results.
- end with shipped, blocked, or needs-Darrin-decision status.

## Finding Disposition

Receiver response must account for every Finding Index item using one of:
- FIXED: [finding title] — [verification summary]
- FALSE POSITIVE: [finding title] — [evidence]
- COVERAGE GAP: [finding title] — [scanner limitation]
- NO CODE CHANGE: [finding title] — [reason]
- DEFERRED: [finding title] — [reason]

LIMITATIONS
----------------------------------------------------------------
  - BA v1.4 static action scanner is heuristic and cannot prove runtime click feedback.
  - External CODEX PG apps other than Panda Agent Hub are statically inspected only; pg_design_lint currently applies to Panda Gallery repo paths in the BA manifest.
  - Runtime Action Feedback v1.0 browser-probes Bible Audit controls only; cross-app PySide click coverage still requires app-specific adapters.
  - Runtime Geometry v1.4 browser-probes Bible Audit only at 1920x1080 and 1000x900; non-BA visual/runtime adapters are still future work.
  - Runtime Check Pack v1.3 wraps PAH Inspector for Panda Agent Hub only; browser visual, PySide click, communication speed trend, and non-PAH runtime adapters are still future work.
